Hyperparameters used are as follows:

batch size = 256, learning rate = 0.03, learning rate decay = 0.97, momentum = 0.9
validation size = 200, dataset expansion multiplier = 0, max images trained = 8000000
loss function = Cross Entropy Loss, optimizer = SGD

dynamic weights based on F1 scores (power of 2), minimum dampening = 0, maximum dampening = 1
initial dampening = 0.1, forward step size = 0.1, reverse step size = 0.04
sample size drop threshold for next dampening step: 0.9

simulation size = 5000, confidence interval used = 95.0 % probability weights correlation = 0.11
probability weights offset = 500 to 5000, probability weights base = 2 to 2
probability weights power = 0 to 19
probability weights for recall = rng(base) ^ rng(power) + rng(offset)
probability weights for precision = (1 - correlation) * (rng(base) ^ rng(power) + rng(offset)) + (correlation * recall)
